SELECT [e].[Id], [e].[ApiUserId], [e].[City], [e].[EndDateTime], [e].[EventCategoryId], [e].[LevelCategoryId], [e].[MaxNumberOfPlayers], [e].[Name], [e].[PriceForEvent], [e].[StartDateTime], [e].[Street], [e].[SurfaceCategoryId], [e].[SurroundingCategoryId], [e0].[Id], [r].[EventId], [r].[ApiUserId], [r].[RegistrationDateTime], [e0].[ImageForBoxWithEventInfo], [e0].[ImageForSearchBar], [e0].[Name]
